$ # First, generate the hash
HASH=$(echo -n "matrixsumlist" | openssl dgst -sha512 | sed 's/.*= //')

# Then, use that hash to decrypt (forcing legacy MD5)

$ # Generate the hash for the long phrase
HASH_LONG=$(echo -n "theflowerblossomsthroughwhatseemstobeaconcretesurface" | openssl dgst -sha512 | sed 's/.*= //')

# Decrypt using the long hash
openssl enc -d -aes-256-cbc -a -md md5 -in cosmic_duality_real.txt -pass pass:$HASH_LONG

$ # -n tells echo NOT to add a newline
HASH=$(echo -n "theflowerblossomsthroughwhatseemstobeaconcretesurface" | openssl dgst -sha512 | sed 's/.*= //')
echo $HASH
# Now try to decrypt with legacy MD5
openssl enc -d -aes-256-cbc -a -md md5 -in cosmic_duality_real.txt -pass pass:$HASH
